<p>1780, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nenets_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Nenets languages">Tundra Nenets</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="yrk">парка</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aleut_language" class="extiw" title="w:Aleut language">Aleut</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ale"><a href = vnd.unilang:parka.html>parka</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">па́рка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">párka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup> Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Uralic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Uralic">Proto-Uralic</a></span>; see dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Finnish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Finnish language">Finnish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fi"><a href = vnd.unilang:parka.html>parka</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rag, swaddling <a href = vnd.unilang:clothes.html>clothes</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which may be cognate from Proto-Uralic, or early borrowing from another <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Uralic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Uralic languages">Uralic</a></span> language.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:parka.html>parka</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">parkas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A long jacket with a hood which protects the wearer against rain and wind.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2002</b> January 3,  James Meek,  <cite>London Review of Books</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Basir tended to wear a <a href = vnd.unilang:beige.html>beige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:suede.html>suede</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:parka.html>parka</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> his shalwar kameez.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***parkiet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:parkiet.html>parkiet</a> (26079)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">perroquet</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">periquito</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">periquito</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:parlement.html>parlement</a> (8168)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:parlement.html>parlement</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:parlement.html>parlement</a></i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parlement.html>parlement</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parlement.html>parlementen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parlement.html>parlementje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">conversation</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">talking</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">discussion</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">talk</span></li>

***parochie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:parochie.html>parochie</a> (12833)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">prochie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">parochia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πᾰροικῐ́ᾱ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paroikíā</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The <i>a</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> usually syncopated in Middle Dutch, but it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> restored and became increasingly common in early modern Dutch due to influence of the Latin term.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parochie.html>parochie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parochies.html>parochies</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">parochiën</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly Roman Catholicism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A parish.</li></ol>

***pas.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a> (327)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:passen.html>passen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:passen.html>passen</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">passus</i>. Equivalent to a derivation from etymology 2.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_4">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>just</li>
<li>hardly</li>
<li>only, not until, not any sooner
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>Pas</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opgeruimd.html>opgeruimd</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:krijg.html>krijg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koekje.html>koekje</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Only</b> when your room <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> cleared up, you'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> get a cookie.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>now ... really
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Da's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoer.html>stoer</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Now</b> that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>really</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:cool.html>cool</a>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></strong> (<i>used only predicatively</i>, <i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>fitting, having a proper fit, having the correct size and shape
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schoenen.html>schoenen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Those <a href = vnd.unilang:shoes.html>shoes</a> do not <b>fit well</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">passus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_11">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:passen.html>passen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pasje.html>pasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>pace, step; also as a measure of distance</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mountain pass</li>
<li>fit of an object, notably depending on forms and/or dimensions</li></ol>

class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish language">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota">آغا‎</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ağa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">master</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> also <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> proposed as etymon.<sup id="cite_ref-Nişanyan_3-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Nişanyan-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pasha.html>pasha</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pashas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A high-ranking Turkish military officer, especially as a commander or regional governor; the highest honorary title during the Ottoman Empire.</li>
<li>The Indian butterfly <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Herona_marathus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Herona marathus"><i>Herona marathus</i></a></span>, family Nymphalidae.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:passen.html>passen</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></i>).

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to try on, to fit, to try for size</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to befit, to suit, to behoove, to be appropriate</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, noun of action from <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> passive participle <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">passus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">suffered</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I <a href = vnd.unilang:suf.html>suffer</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pe(i)<a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span ***pastei.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pastei.html>pastei</a> (17793)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pasteide</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pastei.html>pastei</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pasteien.html>pasteien</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pasteitje.html>pasteitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>savoury pie, pasty <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">often containing meat</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>pâté <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">now chiefly used in compounds</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">paté</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***pastiche.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pastiche.html>pastiche</a> (73635)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>Via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:pastiche.html>pastiche</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">pasticcio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pie, something blended</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*pasticium</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:pasta.html>pasta</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dough, pastry cake, paste</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παστά</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pastá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">barley porridge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παστός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pastós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sprinkled with salt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pastiche.html>pastiche</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pastiches</b>)
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Pastiche.jpg/220px-Pastiche.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="289" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Pastiche.jpg/330px-Pastiche.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Pastiche.jpg/440px-Pastiche.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1505" data-file-height="1975" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Botticelli" class="extiw" title="w:Botticelli">Botticelli</a>'s original on the left, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pastiche.html>pastiche</a></b> on the right. (1)</div></div></div>
<ol><li>A work of art, drama, literature, music, or architecture that imitates the work of a previous artist.</li>
<li>A musical <a href = vnd.unilang:medley.html>medley</a>, typically quoting other works.</li>
<li>An incongruous mixture; a hodgepodge.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A postmodern playwriting technique that fuses a variety of styles, <a href = vnd.unilang:genres.html>genres</a>, and story lines to create a new form.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pastiche.html>pastiche</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">pastiches</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">pastiching</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">pastiched</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To create or compose in a mixture of styles.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2008</b> May 13,  Natalie Angier,  “A Gene Map for the Cute Side of the Family”, in  <cite>New York Times</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/05/13/science/13angi.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">That the genetic code of the platypus proved to be as bizarrely <b>pastiched</b> as its anatomy enhanced the popular appeal of the report, published in the journal Nature.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pastiche.html>pastiche</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:kunst.html>kunst</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> document of <a href = vnd.unilang:ander.html>ander</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunstwerk.html>kunstwerk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoals.html>zoals</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> toneel- of muziekstuk <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemaakt.html>gemaakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> nabootsing <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>/of <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:combineren.html>combineren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bepaalde.html>bepaalde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kenmerken.html>kenmerken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:meerdere.html>meerdere</a> originelen
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:schrijven.html>Schrijven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vorm.html>vorm</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pastiche.html>pastiche</a></b> of <a href = vnd.unilang:parodie.html>parodie</a>.</i> </li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:traditionele.html>Traditionele</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pastiche.html>pastiche</a></b>-architectuur.</i> </li>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">patate</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">patata</i>, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ta%C3%ADno_language" class="extiw" title="w:Taíno language">Taíno</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tnq">batata</i>.

***pater.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pater.html>pater</a> (4486)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:pater.html>pater</a></i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vader.html>vader</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">va</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pater.html>pater</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paters.html>paters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pater.html>patertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>father (in the religious sense)</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pater.html>pater</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
